msg:After climbing through the entire Miao Village, I think the location of this hotel is quite good. The view was also great, so we stayed another night. Many B&Bs in Miao villages are located at the corners of mountain roads. If you are not familiar with the road on the first day, finding your way with your own suitcase will definitely affect your mood during the trip. This B&B has a name on the map of the entire scenic spot. It is an internet celebrity check-in spot. Many girls come to take pictures in the cafe downstairs. Enter the scenic area from the west gate and take the sightseeing bus to Changxiao Station. A butler will pick you up. It is also very convenient to go out for fun, and the station is 20 meters next to it. If you don't take a car, you can quickly walk down the trails and have fun. Highly recommended. The overall service is also very good. On the day we checked out, we needed to take a bus to the North Gate. The North Gate is 40 minutes away from the B&B. The lady at the front desk was very considerate and pushed the box to take us to the Xiaobeimen Station. If you can see the comments, please accept us. Thanks. If I have the chance to come back, I will choose to stay here again.
